title="Worcestershire">Worcestershire</a>\n</td>\n<td>552,900\n</td>\n<td>318/km\xc2\xb2\n</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Wychavon" title="Wychavon">Wychavon</a> (116,300)\n</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Worcester" title="Worcester">Worcester</a> (93,400)\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Warwickshire" title="Warwickshire">Warwickshire</a>\n</td>\n<td>522,200\n</td>\n<td>264/km\xc2\xb2\n</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Warwick_(district)" class="mw-redirect" title="Warwick (district)">Warwick</a> (132,900)\n</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Nuneaton" title="Nuneaton">Nuneaton</a> (70,721)\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Shropshire" title="Shropshire">Shropshire</a>\n</td>\n<td>451,100\n</td>\n<td>129/km\xc2\xb2\n</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Shropshire_Council" title="Shropshire Council">Shropshire</a> (290,900)\n</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Telford" title="Telford">Telford</a> (138,241)\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Herefordshire" title="Herefordshire">Herefordshire</a>\n</td>\n<td>177,800\n</td>\n<td>82/km\xc2\xb2\n</td>\n<td>N/A<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Hereford" title="Hereford">Hereford</a> (50,400)\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>The West Midlands\' population accounts for almost 11% of England\'s overall population. 49.36% of the region\'s population resides in the West Midlands county, 20.17% in Staffordshire, 10.49% in Worcestershire, 9.91% in Warwickshire, 8.56% in Shropshire, and 3.37% in Herefordshire.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=West_Midlands_(region)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=West_Midlands_(region)&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.</span>  <small><i>(January 2017)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG/170px-JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG" width="170" height="199" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG/255px-JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG/340px-JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2604" data-file-height="3043" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:JCB_Chairman_-_Sir_Anthony_Bamford.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Sir Anthony Bamford, the wealthiest British-nationality businessman</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Business_Link" title="Business Link">Business Link</a> West Midlands<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> was based on the Quinton Business Park in <a href="/wiki/Quinton,_Birmingham" title="Quinton, Birmingham">Quinton</a>, next to <a href="/wiki/Highways_England" title="Highways England">Highways England</a> and the M5 at the <a href="/wiki/A456_road" title="A456 road">A456</a> Quinton Interchange. NHS West Midlands, the <a href="/wiki/NHS_strategic_health_authority" class="mw-redirect" title="NHS strategic health authority">strategic health authority</a> was on Hagley Road (A456) in Edgbaston. The <a href="/wiki/West_Midlands_Ambulance_Service" title="West Midlands Ambulance Service">West Midlands Ambulance Service</a> is on the Waterfront Business Park in <a href="/wiki/Brierley_Hill" title="Brierley Hill">Brierley Hill</a>, off the <a href="/wiki/A461_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A461 road">A461</a>, near the headquarters of <a href="/wiki/West_Midlands_Police" title="West Midlands Police">West Midlands Police</a>, where the <a href="/wiki/Child_Support_Agency" title="Child Support Agency">Child Support Agency</a> (CSA) was headquartered. The region\'s <a href="/wiki/Manufacturing_Advisory_Service" title="Manufacturing Advisory Service">Manufacturing Advisory Service</a> was on <a href="/w/index.php?title=Wolverhampton_Science_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Wolverhampton Science Park (page does not exist)">Wolverhampton Science Park</a><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> off the <a href="/wiki/A449_road" title="A449 road">A449</a> north of the city centre; this function is now represented by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Made_in_the_Midlands&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Made in the Midlands (page does not exist)">Made in the Midlands</a>, off M4 junction 2 at Pendeford north of Wolverhampton. The <a href="/wiki/Department_for_International_Trade" title="Department for International Trade">DIT</a> West Midlands (previously <a href="/wiki/UK_Trade_%26_Investment" title="UK Trade &amp; Investment">UKTI</a>) for the region<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> is based at the <a href="/wiki/West_Midlands_Chambers_of_Commerce" title="West Midlands Chambers of Commerce">West Midlands Chambers of Commerce</a> on <i>Harborne Road</i> (B4284), south of NHS West Midlands west of Five Ways; this was previously at the B4100/B4114 junction south of Aston University near the Matthew Boulton Campus of <a href="/wiki/Birmingham_Metropolitan_College" title="Birmingham Metropolitan College">Birmingham Metropolitan College</a>. Most of the region is covered by the <a href="/wiki/Midlands_Air_Ambulance" title="Midlands Air Ambulance">Midlands Air Ambulance</a>, except Warwickshire is covered by the <a href="/wiki/Warwickshire_%26_Northamptonshire_Air_Ambulance" class="mw-redirect" title="Warwickshire &amp; Northamptonshire Air Ambulance">Warwickshire &amp; Northamptonshire Air Ambulance</a>, based at <a href="/wiki/Coventry_Airport" title="Coventry Airport">Coventry Airport</a>; both are charity-funded. Sir <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Bamford" title="Anthony Bamford">Anthony Bamford</a> of Staffordshire is the richest British industrialist, at around \xc2\xa33.15bn in 2014; Sir <a href="/wiki/James_Dyson" title="James Dyson">James Dyson</a> is second (\xc2\xa33bn).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Herefordshire">Herefordshire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=West_Midlands_(region)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Herefordshire">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg/220px-Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg" width="220" height="137" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg/330px-Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg/440px-Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="398" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Cider_orchards_east_of_Hereford_2_-_geograph.org.uk_-_899483.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Bulmers cider orchard east of Hereford, near the <a href="/wiki/River_Wye" title="River Wye">River Wye</a></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/H._P._Bulmer" title="H. P. Bulmer">Bulmers Cider</a> is in Hereford within walking distance of <a href="/wiki/Hereford_railway_station" title="Hereford railway station">Hereford station</a>; it is the world\'s largest <a href="/wiki/Cider" title="Cider">cider</a> factory, and has the world\'s largest vat (for <a href="/wiki/Strongbow_(cider)" title="Strongbow (cider)">Strongbow</a>), built in 1975. <a href="/wiki/Painter_Brothers" title="Painter Brothers">Painter Brothers</a> (part of <a href="/wiki/Balfour_Beatty" title="Balfour Beatty">Balfour Beatty</a>) on the Aydon Ind Est off the A49 near <a href="/wiki/Hereford_Racecourse" title="Hereford Racecourse">Hereford Racecourse</a> in the north of Hereford, is the UK\'s largest manufacturer of electricity pylons (<a href="/wiki/Transmission_tower" title="Transmission tower">transmission towers</a>), <a href="/wiki/Radio_masts_and_towers" title="Radio masts and towers">broadcasting masts</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Callender-Hamilton_bridge" title="Callender-Hamilton bridge">Callender-Hamilton bridge</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Railway_electrification_in_Great_Britain" title="Railway electrification in Great Britain">rail electrification</a> structures. <a href="/wiki/Henry_Wiggin" title="Henry Wiggin">Special Metals Wiggin</a>, part of <a href="/wiki/Special_Metals_Corporation" title="Special Metals Corporation">Special Metals Corporation</a>, based at Hereford was the main producer of <a href="/wiki/List_of_alloys" title="List of alloys">nickel alloys</a> in Europe, with a large site directly north of Painter Brothers at the A49/A4103 junction; further north on the A49 at Moreton Business Park at <a href="/wiki/Moreton-on-Lugg" title="Moreton-on-Lugg">Moreton-on-Lugg</a> is GEA Denco (part of <a href="/wiki/GEA_Group" title="GEA Group">GEA Group</a>) who make <a href="/wiki/Dehumidifier" title="Dehumidifier">dehumidifiers</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Special_Reconnaissance_Regiment" title="Special Reconnaissance Regiment">Special Reconnaissance Regiment</a> was formed in 2005. At Hereford, <a href="/wiki/Cargill_Meat_Solutions" title="Cargill Meat Solutions">Cargill Meats Europe</a> (formerly Sun Valley) have a large poultry meat processing facility, processing chickens from around Herefordshire; it produces a lot of the chicken for <a href="/wiki/McDonald%27s" title="McDonald&#39;s">McDonald\'s</a> in the UK and processes around a million birds a week.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Cadbury" title="Cadbury">Cadbury</a> (Mondel\xc4\x93z International) make milk chocolate crumb near <a href="/wiki/Marlbrook,_Herefordshire" title="Marlbrook, Herefordshire">Marlbrook</a> (near <a href="/wiki/Leominster" title="Leominster">Leominster</a>). <a href="/wiki/Weston%27s_Cider" title="Weston&#39;s Cider">Weston\'s Cider</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Much_Marcle" title="Much Marcle">Much Marcle</a>, south-west of <a href="/wiki/Ledbury" title="Ledbury">Ledbury</a> at the <a href="/wiki/A449_road" title="A449 road">A449</a>/B4024 junction, who also make Stowford Press. Wye Fruit is in the north of Ledbury on the B4214; in the west of the town, off the <a href="/wiki/A417_road" title="A417 road">A417</a> bypass is a large site of <a href="/wiki/Amcor" title="Amcor">Amcor</a>, and further west is Universal Beverages (UBL), owned by Heineken since 2007 where it cans cider; the site of Ledbury Preserves of RHM made <a href="/wiki/Robertson%27s" title="Robertson&#39;s">Robertson\'s</a> jam, mincemeat and marmalade and closed in 2008 when production moved to <a href="/wiki/Histon_and_Impington" title="Histon and Impington">Histon</a> in Cambridgeshire. <a href="/wiki/Atora" title="Atora">Atora</a> suet has been made in Ledbury since around 2003, when production was moved from Teesside by RHM to a former factory of <a href="/wiki/Just_Juice" class="mw-redirect" title="Just Juice">Just Juice</a>, which was bought by <a href="/wiki/Del_Monte_Foods" title="Del Monte Foods">Del Monte</a> in 1999.  Holden Aluminium Technologies are a sports car chassis manufacturer at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Linton,_Bringsty&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Linton, Bringsty (page does not exist)">Linton</a> on the <a href="/wiki/A44_road" title="A44 road">A44</a>, east of <a href="/wiki/Bromyard" title="Bromyard">Bromyard</a>. <a href="/wiki/Kingspan_Group" title="Kingspan Group">Kingspan Insulation</a> is based at <a href="/wiki/Pembridge" title="Pembridge">Pembridge</a>, next to <a href="/wiki/Shobdon_Aerodrome" title="Shobdon Aerodrome">Shobdon Aerodrome</a>, west of Leominster off the A44. BT\'s <a href="/wiki/Madley_Communications_Centre" title="Madley Communications Centre">Madley Communications Centre</a>, claims to be the world\'s largest <a href="/wiki/Ground_station" title="Ground station">earth station</a>. <a href="/wiki/Tyrrells_(crisps)" title="Tyrrells (crisps)">Tyrrells Potato Crisps</a> are off the B4457 at <a href="/wiki/Dilwyn" title="Dilwyn">Dilwyn</a> west of Leominster, near the A44.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Shropshire">Shropshire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=West_Midlands_(region)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Shropshire">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Rayburn_Range" class="mw-redirect" title="Rayburn Range">Rayburn Range</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aga_Rangemaster_Group" title="Aga Rangemaster Group">Aga Rangemaster Group</a> are based in <a href="/wiki/Telford" title="Telford">Telford</a>; the <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Dispensary_for_Sick_Animals" title="People&#39;s Dispensary for Sick Animals">PDSA</a> is in <a href="/wiki/St_George%27s_and_Priorslee" title="St George&#39;s and Priorslee">St George\'s and Priorslee</a>, Telford next to the M54 near the B5061/A5 Priorslee Roundabout; opposite the M54 on Stafford Park is <a href="/wiki/Virgin_Balloon_Flights" title="Virgin Balloon Flights">Virgin Balloon Flights</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hymix&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hymix (page does not exist)">Hymix</a> is on the east of Stafford Park near the A464, who make mountable <a href="/wiki/Concrete_mixer" title="Concrete mixer">concrete mixers</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(United_Kingdom)" title="Ministry of Defence (United Kingdom)">MoD</a> have a significant depot at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lilleshall_and_Donnington&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lilleshall and Donnington (page does not exist)">Lilleshall and Donnington</a>. There are also high-technology industries such as <a href="/wiki/Unimation" title="Unimation">Unimation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nikon" title="Nikon">Nikon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hitachi_Maxell" class="mw-redirect" title="Hitachi Maxell">Hitachi Maxell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ricoh" title="Ricoh">Ricoh</a>, <a href="/wiki/Capgemini" title="Capgemini">Capgemini</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fujitsu" title="Fujitsu">Fujitsu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Electronic_Data_Systems" title="Electronic Data Systems">Electronic Data Systems</a>. In <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hadley_Castle&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hadley Castle (page does not exist)">Hadley Castle</a> off the A442, <a href="/wiki/Denso" title="Denso">Denso</a> Manufacturing UK Ltd make <a href="/wiki/Car_air_conditioning" class="mw-redirect" title="Car air conditioning">car air-conditioning systems</a> and <a href="/wiki/GKN" title="GKN">GKN</a> Wheels make car wheels. Nearby is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ogihara_Corporation&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ogihara Corporation (page does not exist)">Ogihara</a> Europe, a tool making (<a href="/wiki/Die_(manufacturing)" title="Die (manufacturing)">dies</a> and <a href="/wiki/Machine_press" title="Machine press">press</a>) and metal-pressing company. <a href="/wiki/Makita" title="Makita">Makita</a> Manufacturing Europe off the <a href="/wiki/A518_road" title="A518 road">A518</a> at Hortonwood at Telford is the only plant in the UK that makes <a href="/wiki/Power_tool" title="Power tool">power tools</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Chequer_Foods&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Chequer Foods (page does not exist)">Chequer Foods</a> (owned by the Chiswick-based <a href="/w/index.php?title=Autobar_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Autobar Group (page does not exist)">Autobar Group</a>), off the A442 near the A4169 junction in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Halesfield&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Halesfield (page does not exist)">Halesfield</a> to the south, make food sachets for foodservice and for the <a href="/wiki/Operational_Ration_Pack" class="mw-redirect" title="Operational Ration Pack">UK\'s military ration packs</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/M%C3%BCller_(company)" title="M\xc3\xbcller (company)">M\xc3\xbcller Dairy Ltd</a> is based in <a href="/wiki/Market_Drayton" title="Market Drayton">Market Drayton</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Palethorpes" title="Palethorpes">Palethorpes</a>, part of <a href="/wiki/Pork_Farms" title="Pork Farms">Pork Farms</a> which makes own-label sausages, is on the same site on <a href="/wiki/A53_road" title="A53 road">A53</a>. At <a href="/wiki/Crudgington" title="Crudgington">Crudgington</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dairy_Crest" title="Dairy Crest">Dairy Crest</a> made <i>Country Life</i> butter and <a href="/wiki/Clover_(spread)" title="Clover (spread)">Clover</a> until February 2015, and have their Technical Centre. Anglo Beef Processors (<a href="/w/index.php?title=ABP_Food_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ABP Food Group (page does not exist)">ABP Food Group</a>) are at <a href="/wiki/Harlescott" title="Harlescott">Harlescott</a> in the north of Shrewsbury. Nearby <a href="/w/index.php?title=Stadco&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Stadco (page does not exist)">Stadco</a>, a metal pressings company, are based off the A5124 and next to the railway, on the <a href="/wiki/Battlefield,_Shropshire" title="Battlefield, Shropshire">Battlefield</a> Ind Estate and have a site at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hadley_Castle&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Hadley Castle (page does not exist)">Hadley Castle</a>, Telford off the <a href="/wiki/A442_road" title="A442 road">A442</a>. <a href="/wiki/Uniq_plc" title="Uniq plc">Uniq plc</a> have a plant on the <a href="/wiki/A488_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A488 road">A488</a> at <a href="/wiki/Minsterley" title="Minsterley">Minsterley</a> making chilled desserts for Tesco.\n</p><p>BT have their <a href="/wiki/National_Network_Management_Centre" title="National Network Management Centre">National Network Management Centre</a> (Whittington House) off the A495 near the A5 roundabout on the Oswestry bypass in <a href="/wiki/Whittington,_Shropshire" title="Whittington, Shropshire">Whittington, Shropshire</a>, where they claim to have the largest video information wall in Europe.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Military helicopter training in the UK takes place at <a href="/wiki/RAF_Shawbury" title="RAF Shawbury">RAF Shawbury</a>, alongside training for the RAF\'s <a href="/wiki/Air_traffic_controller" title="Air traffic controller">air traffic controllers</a> (ATC).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Staffordshire">Staffordshire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=West_Midlands_(region)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Staffordshire">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre,_Gaydon.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre%2C_Gaydon.jpg/220px-JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre%2C_Gaydon.jpg" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre%2C_Gaydon.jpg/330px-JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre%2C_Gaydon.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre%2C_Gaydon.jpg/440px-JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre%2C_Gaydon.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1362" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:JCB_Diesel_Max_Heritage_Motor_Centre,_Gaydon.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/JCB_Dieselmax" title="JCB Dieselmax">JCB Dieselmax</a>, holder of the <a href="/wiki/Land_speed_record" title="Land speed record">land speed record</a> for diesel-engined vehicles</div></div></div>\n<p>The brewing companies such as <a href="/wiki/Molson_Coors_Brewing_Company" title="Molson Coors Brewing Company">Coors Brewers</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Burton_on_Trent" class="mw-redirect" title="Burton on Trent">Burton on Trent</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/Marmite" title="Marmite">Marmite</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marston%27s_Brewery" title="Marston&#39;s Brewery">Marston\'s Brewery</a>, <a href="/wiki/General_Nutrition_Centers" class="mw-redirect" title="General Nutrition Centers">GNC UK</a> (<a href="/wiki/Dietary_supplement" title="Dietary supplement">health supplements</a>), and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Doncasters&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Doncasters (page does not exist)">Doncasters</a> (aerospace components and steel <a href="/wiki/Forging" title="Forging">forging</a>, founded by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Daniel_Doncaster&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Daniel Doncaster (page does not exist)">Daniel Doncaster</a> of Sheffield). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Conder_Structures&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Conder Structures (page does not exist)">Conder Structures</a> is a structural steel company next to Marmite on the A5121, and further south <a href="/wiki/Johnson_Controls" title="Johnson Controls">Johnson Controls</a> make seats for Toyota in <a href="/wiki/Branston,_Staffordshire" title="Branston, Staffordshire">Branston</a>. <a href="/wiki/Spirit_Pub_Company" title="Spirit Pub Company">Spirit Pub Company</a> (which demerged from Punch Taverns in August 2011, and owns <a href="/wiki/Chef_%26_Brewer" title="Chef &amp; Brewer">Chef &amp; Brewer</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Flaming_Grill&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Flaming Grill (page does not exist)">Flaming Grill</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Fayre_%26_Square&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Fayre &amp; Square (page does not exist)">Fayre &amp; Square</a>) is near the A5121/A38 junction, with <a href="/wiki/Punch_Taverns" title="Punch Taverns">Punch Taverns</a> slightly further north. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Marley_Eternit&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Marley Eternit (page does not exist)">Marley Eternit</a> (part of the Belgium <a href="/wiki/Fibre_cement" title="Fibre cement">fibre cement</a> roofing (often seen on industrial buildings) are based on the west side of the A38 in the south of Branston, (with another large plant at the <a href="/wiki/A525_road" title="A525 road">A525</a>/<a href="/wiki/A531_road" title="A531 road">A531</a> junction in <a href="/wiki/Madeley,_Staffordshire" title="Madeley, Staffordshire">Madeley</a> near the M6 at <a href="/wiki/Keele" title="Keele">Keele</a>); next door in <a href="/wiki/Dunstall" title="Dunstall">Dunstall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lanxess" title="Lanxess">Lanxess</a> UK (former W. Hawley) make pigments.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Roundabout_by_Michelin_Factory_-_geograph.org.uk_-_336395.jpg" bibendum</i></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Newell_Rubbermaid" class="mw-redirect" title="Newell Rubbermaid">Newell Rubbermaid</a> UK (owner of <a href="/wiki/Parker_Pen_Company" title="Parker Pen Company">Parker Pen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Berol" title="Berol">Berol</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paper_Mate" title="Paper Mate">Paper Mate</a> and <a href="/wiki/DYMO_Corporation" title="DYMO Corporation">DYMO</a>), <a href="/wiki/Graco_(baby_products)" title="Graco (baby products)">Graco</a> (<a href="/wiki/Baby_transport" title="Baby transport">buggies</a>), a large <a href="/wiki/Distribution_center" title="Distribution center">RDC</a> of Tesco, and <a href="/wiki/Zytek" class="mw-redirect" title="Zytek">Zytek</a> (motorsport) are at <a href="/wiki/Fradley" title="Fradley">Fradley</a> Park, next to the A38, on an <a href="/wiki/RAF_Lichfield" title="RAF Lichfield">old airfield</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norgren_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Norgren (company) (page does not exist)">Norgren</a> (part of IMI) is an international <a href="/wiki/Pneumatics" title="Pneumatics">pneumatic</a> technology company on the A5192 in Lichfield.\n</p><p>Off the A522 north of Cheadle is JCB Earthmovers (<a href="/wiki/Loader_(equipment)" title="Loader (equipment)">wheel loaders</a>) and JCB Compact Products (mini excavators and <a href="/wiki/Skid-steer_loader" title="Skid-steer loader">skid-steer loaders</a>). <a href="/wiki/JCB_(company)" title="JCB (company)">JCB</a> is based in Staffordshire, near the <a href="/wiki/Alton_Towers" title="Alton Towers">Alton Towers</a> colossal leisure park; JCB Heavy Products (excavators), and their World Parts Centre are off the A50 in <a href="/wiki/Uttoxeter_Rural" title="Uttoxeter Rural">Uttoxeter Rural</a> (<a href="/wiki/Beamhurst" title="Beamhurst">Beamhurst</a>). Lafarge Cement UK (former <a href="/wiki/Blue_Circle_Industries" title="Blue Circle Industries">Blue Circle</a>) have a large plant at <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cauldon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cauldon (page does not exist)">Cauldon</a> in <a href="/wiki/Waterhouses,_Staffordshire" title="Waterhouses, Staffordshire">Waterhouses</a>, between the A523 and A52.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Michelin" title="Michelin">Michelin</a> Tyres are made in <a href="/wiki/Sideway" title="Sideway">Sideway</a> in Stoke-on-Trent, next to Stoke\'s only <a href="/wiki/St_Joseph%27s_College,_Stoke-on-Trent" title="St Joseph&#39;s College, Stoke-on-Trent">grammar school</a> in the south of <a href="/wiki/Trent_Vale" title="Trent Vale">Trent Vale</a>. <a href="/wiki/Royal_Doulton" title="Royal Doulton">Royal Doulton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wedgwood" title="Wedgwood">Wedgwood</a> are based in <a href="/wiki/Barlaston" title="Barlaston">Barlaston</a>. <a href="/wiki/Emma_Bridgewater" title="Emma Bridgewater">Emma Bridgewater</a> make pottery on the A50 in Hanley. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Tile_Giant&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tile Giant (page does not exist)">Tile Giant</a> (owned by Travis Perkins since 2007) is based on the B5039 in Longton, and <a href="/wiki/Walkers%27_Nonsuch" title="Walkers&#39; Nonsuch">Walkers\' Nonsuch</a> make toffee on the A5007. <a href="/wiki/Portmeirion_Pottery" title="Portmeirion Pottery">Portmeirion Pottery</a>, who own the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Worcester" title="Royal Worcester">Royal Worcester</a> brand, are on the B5041 in Stoke. <a href="/wiki/Steelite_International" class="mw-redirect" title="Steelite International">Steelite International</a> (pottery) are based at <a href="/wiki/Middleport,_Staffordshire" title="Middleport, Staffordshire">Middleport</a>, in west Burslem, next to the <a href="/wiki/Trent_and_Mersey_Canal" title="Trent and Mersey Canal">Trent and Mersey Canal</a>. <a href="/wiki/Dudson" title="Dudson">Dudson</a> (pottery) is on the A50 in the north end of Burslem, towards Tunstall. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Johnson_Tiles&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Johnson Tiles (page does not exist)">Johnson Tiles</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norcros_Adhesives&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Norcros Adhesives (page does not exist)">Norcros Adhesives</a> (owned by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Norcros&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Norcros (page does not exist)">Norcros</a>) is in the west of Tunstall. <a href="/wiki/Wade_Ceramics" title="Wade Ceramics">Wade Ceramics</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Etruria,_Staffordshire" title="Etruria, Staffordshire">Etruria</a> to the east of Wolstanton, near the A53/A500 junction off the A53, near the HQ of the Sentinel newspaper (<a href="/wiki/DMG_Media" title="DMG Media">Harmsworth Printing</a>). <a href="/w/index.php?title=Swan_Products&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Swan Products (page does not exist)">Swan Products</a> (<a href="/wiki/Teasmade" title="Teasmade">teasmades</a> and small appliances, owned by Littlewoods) are based in <a href="/wiki/Fenton,_Staffordshire" title="Fenton, Staffordshire">Fenton</a>. <a href="/wiki/Premier_Foods" title="Premier Foods">Premier Foods</a> make <a href="/wiki/Mr_Kipling" title="Mr Kipling">Mr Kipling</a> slices and <a href="/wiki/Bakewell_tart" title="Bakewell tart">Cherry Bakewells</a> in Trent Vale in the south of Stoke-on-Trent.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Bet365" title="Bet365">Bet365</a> is on <a href="/wiki/Stoke-on-Trent_Garden_Festival" title="Stoke-on-Trent Garden Festival">Festival Park</a> in <a href="/wiki/Etruria,_Staffordshire" title="Etruria, Staffordshire">Etruria</a>, off the <a href="/wiki/A53_road" title="A53 road">A53</a>, and is Stoke-on-Trent\'s largest private sector employer. <a href="/wiki/Goodwin_Steel_Castings" title="Goodwin Steel Castings">Goodwin Steel Castings</a> make steel <a href="/wiki/Casting_(metalworking)" title="Casting (metalworking)">castings</a> in the east of Stoke on the A52. <a href="/wiki/The_Co-operative_Pharmacy" class="mw-redirect" title="The Co-operative Pharmacy">The Co-operative Pharmacy</a> National Distribution Centre is on the A50 at <a href="/wiki/Meir,_Staffordshire" title="Meir, Staffordshire">Meir</a>, on the former site of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cookson_Ceramics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cookson Ceramics (page does not exist)">Cookson Ceramics</a> (later <a href="/wiki/Johnson_Matthey" title="Johnson Matthey">Johnson Matthey</a> until its closure in 2003). <a href="/wiki/Dechra_Pharmaceuticals" title="Dechra Pharmaceuticals">Dechra Pharmaceuticals</a> make <a href="/wiki/Veterinary_pharmacist" title="Veterinary pharmacist">veterinary pharmaceuticals</a> at <a href="/wiki/Talke" title="Talke">Talke</a>, off the A34. <a href="/wiki/Churchill_China" title="Churchill China">Churchill China</a> are at Sandyford near <a href="/wiki/Tunstall,_Staffordshire" title="Tunstall, Staffordshire">Tunstall</a> at the A50/<a href="/wiki/A527_road" title="A527 road">A527</a> junction. <a href="/wiki/Sumitomo_Corporation" title="Sumitomo Corporation">Sumitomo Electrical Wiring Systems (Europe)</a>, who supply wiring for the automotive industry, are in <a href="/wiki/Silverdale,_Staffordshire" title="Silverdale, Staffordshire">Silverdale</a>, not far from <a href="/wiki/Keele_University" title="Keele University">Keele University</a>. At <a href="/wiki/Kidsgrove" title="Kidsgrove">Kidsgrove</a> off the A34, <a href="/wiki/Converteam" class="mw-redirect" title="Converteam">Converteam</a> (former GEC) make <a href="/wiki/Adjustable-speed_drive" title="Adjustable-speed drive">variable speed drives</a> (VSDs); AAH Pharmaceuticals have their Enterprise and Trident divisions in <a href="/wiki/Talke" title="Talke">Talke</a>, in the west of Kidsgrove, off the <a href="/wiki/A5011_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A5011 road">A5011</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=AWS_Electronics&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="AWS Electronics (page does not exist)">AWS Electronics</a> have a factory, off the A34 north of Newcastle. <a href="/wiki/Phones_4u" title="Phones 4u">Phones 4u</a> was at <a href="/wiki/Knutton" title="Knutton">Knutton</a> in the north of <a href="/wiki/Borough_of_Newcastle-under-Lyme" title="Borough of Newcastle-under-Lyme">Newcastle-under-Lyme</a> until it went bankrupt in 2014. Off the B5500 in <a href="/wiki/Chesterton,_Staffordshire" title="Chesterton, Staffordshire">Chesterton</a> in the north-west of Newcastle, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Broxap&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Broxap (page does not exist)">Broxap</a> are a leading supplier of <a href="/wiki/Cast_iron" title="Cast iron">cast iron</a> <a href="/wiki/Street_furniture" title="Street furniture">street furniture</a>. <a href="/wiki/Andritz_AG" title="Andritz AG">Andritz</a> UK (engineering) are at Wolstanton, off the A34 in the north of Newcastle.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG/220px-Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG/330px-Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG/440px-Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2592" data-file-height="3888" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Marmite-Guinness_edition.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Marmite is made from the <a href="/wiki/Yeast_extract" title="Yeast extract">yeast left over</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Beer_in_England" title="Beer in England">brewing industry</a></div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/RoadChef" class="mw-redirect" title="RoadChef">RoadChef</a> are at <a href="/wiki/Norton_Canes" title="Norton Canes">Norton Canes</a>, near <a href="/wiki/Cannock" title="Cannock">Cannock</a>. Tallent Automotive (previously <a href="/wiki/ThyssenKrupp" title="ThyssenKrupp">ThyssenKrupp</a>, now owned by <a href="/wiki/Gestamp_Automoci%C3%B3n" title="Gestamp Automoci\xc3\xb3n">Gestamp</a> since 2011) make <a href="/wiki/Suspension_(vehicle)" title="Suspension (vehicle)">car suspensions</a> and <a href="/wiki/Crossmember" title="Crossmember">crossmembers</a> at Cannock. <a href="/wiki/Electrium" title="Electrium">Electrium</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=Wylex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Wylex (page does not exist)">Wylex</a> <a href="/wiki/Residual-current_device" title="Residual-current device">RCDs</a>, and Crabtree and Volex electrical wiring) is on the A460 next to the M6 toll at <a href="/wiki/Bridgtown" title="Bridgtown">Bridgtown</a>. <a href="/wiki/Mann%2BHummel" title="Mann+Hummel">Mann+Hummel</a> UK, on the A460 south of M54 junction 1 at <a href="/wiki/Featherstone,_Staffordshire" title="Featherstone, Staffordshire">Featherstone</a>, make <a href="/wiki/Air_filter" title="Air filter">air</a> and <a href="/wiki/Oil_filter" title="Oil filter">oil filters</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Motivair&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Motivair (page does not exist)">Motivair</a>, who make <a href="/wiki/Air_compressor" title="Air compressor">air compressors</a>, is based off the A5190 in <a href="/wiki/Burntwood" title="Burntwood">Burntwood</a>; <a href="/wiki/Mizkan" title="Mizkan">Mizkan</a> Europe (who now own <a href="/wiki/Branston_(brand)" title="Branston (brand)">Branston Pickle</a> in Suffolk) make vinegar. Armitage Shanks (owned by <a href="/wiki/Ideal_Standard" title="Ideal Standard">Ideal Standard</a> International) are in the east of Rugeley off the A513 in <a href="/wiki/Armitage_with_Handsacre" title="Armitage with Handsacre">Armitage with Handsacre</a>, near the WCML; JCB Cab Systems are next to the A51 on the Riverside Ind Est.\n</p><p>The UK headquarters of <a href="/wiki/Alstom" title="Alstom">Alstom</a> Grid (former <a href="/wiki/Areva" class="mw-redirect" title="Areva">Areva</a> T&amp;D UK, and <a href="/wiki/General_Electric_Company_plc" class="mw-redirect" title="General Electric Company plc">GEC</a>) is based in <a href="/wiki/Stafford" title="Stafford">Stafford</a> as well as a factory and the UK headquarters of <a href="/wiki/Bostik" title="Bostik">Bostik</a> (a subsidiary of <a href="/wiki/Total_S.A." title="Total S.A.">TOTAL</a>). Alstom Power repair electrical generators. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Altecnic&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Altecnic (page does not exist)">Altecnic</a>, who work with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Caleffi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Caleffi (page does not exist)">Caleffi</a> of Italy, is in the north of Stafford in <a href="/wiki/Creswell,_Staffordshire" title="Creswell, Staffordshire">Creswell</a>, off M6 junction 14, and supply <a href="/wiki/Piping_and_plumbing_fitting" title="Piping and plumbing fitting">plumbing fittings</a>. MICROMINIATURES on the B5026 in Stone claim to be Europe\'s leading supplier of <a href="/wiki/Ice_cream_van" title="Ice cream van">ice cream van</a> chime equipment.\n</p><p><a href="/w/index.php?title=Invotec_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Invotec Group (page does not exist)">Invotec Group</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Printed_circuit_board" title="Printed circuit board">PCB</a> manufacturer, is based off the A51 in <a href="/wiki/Dosthill" title="Dosthill">Dosthill</a>, south of Tamworth. <a href="/wiki/Numark_(pharmacy)" title="Numark (pharmacy)">Numark Pharmacy</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Tamworth,_Staffordshire" title="Tamworth, Staffordshire">Tamworth</a> (former base of <a href="/wiki/Reliant" class="mw-redirect" title="Reliant">Reliant</a>). JVM Castings make <a href="/wiki/Crankcase" title="Crankcase">crankcases</a> off the A51 at The Leys in Tamworth, and have a site in Worcester. <a href="/wiki/Bristan" title="Bristan">Bristan</a> (owned by <a href="/wiki/Masco" title="Masco">Masco</a>) based in <a href="/wiki/Dordon" title="Dordon">Dordon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Baddesley_Ensor" title="Baddesley Ensor">Baddesley Ensor</a> on the Birch Coppice Business Park south-west of Tamworth, next to a new <a href="/wiki/Ocado" title="Ocado">Ocado</a> distribution centre, is the UK\'s largest supplier of kitchen and bathroom taps; Volkswagen Group (VAG UK) have their main UK distribution facility there, the site of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Birch_Coppice_Colliery&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Birch Coppice Colliery (page does not exist)">Birch Coppice Colliery</a> before 1987; nearby <a href="/wiki/Maersk" title="Maersk">Maersk</a> have their <a href="/w/index.php?title=Birmingham_Intermodal_Freight_Terminal&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Birmingham Intermodal Freight Terminal (page does not exist)">Birmingham Intermodal Freight Terminal</a> (rail). <a href="/wiki/Ansell" title="Ansell">Ansell</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Medical_glove" title="Medical glove">medical gloves</a>, from Australia) is on Tamworth Enterprise Park, off the A51 next to the West Coast Main Line; they also produce <a href="/wiki/Mates_condoms" title="Mates condoms">Mates condoms</a>. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lyalvale_Express&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lyalvale Express (page does not exist)">Lyalvale Express</a> make <a href="/wiki/Shotgun_shell" title="Shotgun shell">shotgun cartridges</a> north of Tamworth next to the WCML at <a href="/wiki/Fisherwick" title="Fisherwick">Fisherwick</a>. <a href="/wiki/Whittington_Barracks" title="Whittington Barracks">Whittington Barracks</a> (DMS Whittington) near to the west is the home of the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Medical_Services" title="Defence Medical Services">Defence Medical Services</a> and <a href="/wiki/Defence_Dental_Service" title="Defence Dental Service">Defence Dental Service</a>, and soon the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Medical_Services_Training_Centre" class="mw-redirect" title="Defence Medical Services Training Centre">Defence Medical Services Training Centre</a>.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Premier_Foods" title="Premier Foods">Premier Foods</a> make <a href="/wiki/Bird%27s_Custard" title="Bird&#39;s Custard">Bird\'s Custard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Angel_Delight" title="Angel Delight">Angel Delight</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marvel_(food)" title="Marvel (food)">Marvel</a> <a href="/wiki/Powdered_milk" title="Powdered milk">powdered milk</a> in <a href="/wiki/Knighton,_Stafford,_Staffordshire" title="Knighton, Stafford, Staffordshire">Knighton</a>, west of <a href="/wiki/Eccleshall" title="Eccleshall">Eccleshall</a> near the Shropshire boundary. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Static_Systems_Group&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Static Systems Group (page does not exist)">Static Systems Group</a> (SSG) in Wombourne, south Staffordshire, make most of the <a href="/wiki/Nurse_call_button" title="Nurse call button">nurse call</a> systems for the NHS. Kerrygold have a large cheese production site on the <a href="/wiki/A53_road" title="A53 road">A53</a> in <a href="/wiki/Leek,_Staffordshire" title="Leek, Staffordshire">Leek</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Barnfields" title="Barnfields">Barnfields</a> Industrial Estate.\n</p><p>On the Balliol Business Park, in <a href="/wiki/Bilbrook,_Staffordshire" title="Bilbrook, Staffordshire">Bilbrook</a> and directly west of Fordhouses in Wolverhampton north of <a href="/wiki/Pendeford" title="Pendeford">Pendeford</a>, Cargill process poultry (with another site at Hereford), and next door is <a href="/wiki/Moog_Inc." title="Moog Inc.">Moog Aircraft</a> (<a href="/wiki/GE_Aviation" title="GE Aviation">GE Aviation</a> Systems before September 2009, which had bought <a href="/wiki/Smiths_Aerospace" class="mw-redirect" title="Smiths Aerospace">Smiths Aerospace</a> in May 2007) which makes <a href="/wiki/Aircraft_flight_control_system" title="Aircraft flight control system">flight control</a> actuation systems (for the hydraulics on Boeing and Airbus), to move to the <a href="/wiki/I54" title="I54">I54</a> Business Park in Bilbrook; the Balliol Business Park was formerly the site of <a href="/wiki/Boulton_Paul_Aircraft" title="Boulton Paul Aircraft">Boulton Paul Aircraft</a>, that made the <a href="/wiki/Boulton_Paul_Defiant" title="Boulton Paul Defiant">Defiant</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Warwickshire">Warwickshire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a at Warwick</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Bridgestone" title="Bridgestone">Bridgestone</a> UK, <a href="/wiki/Telent" title="Telent">Telent</a> (near the A46 bypass), <a href="/wiki/Calor_Gas" title="Calor Gas">Calor</a> (on Tachbrook Park off the <a href="/wiki/A452_road" title="A452 road">A452</a>), next to <a href="/wiki/Co-operative_Energy" class="mw-redirect" title="Co-operative Energy">Co-operative Energy</a> and near <a href="/wiki/Magna_Powertrain" title="Magna Powertrain">Magna Powertrain</a> UK, <a href="/wiki/Baxi" title="Baxi">Baxi</a> (now owned by <a href="/wiki/BDR_Thermea" title="BDR Thermea">BDR Thermea</a>, and on the A429 near <a href="/wiki/Warwick_railway_station" title="Warwick railway station">Warwick railway station</a>) with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Potterton_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Potterton (company) (page does not exist)">Potterton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Volvo_Trucks" title="Volvo Trucks">Volvo Trucks</a> UK (next to the A46 bypass) and a large data centre of <a href="/wiki/IBM" title="IBM">IBM</a> are in <a href="/wiki/Warwick" title="Warwick">Warwick</a>. <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Eagle" title="Dennis Eagle">Dennis Eagle</a>, who make bin wagons, are headquartered off the A452 on the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Heathcote,_Warwickshire&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Heathcote, Warwickshire (page does not exist)">Heathcote</a> Ind Estate, south of Calor Gas, in east Warwick towards Leamington. <a href="/wiki/Godiva_Fire_Pumps" title="Godiva Fire Pumps">Godiva</a> (former Hale Products Europe, part of the <a href="/wiki/IDEX_Corporation" title="IDEX Corporation">IDEX Corporation</a>) are the UK\'s leading manufacturer of <a href="/wiki/Fire_pump" title="Fire pump">fire pumps</a> off the <a href="/wiki/A445_road" title="A445 road">A445</a> in <a href="/w/index.php?title=Emscote&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Emscote (page does not exist)">Emscote</a>, east Warwick.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:IBM_Warwick_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1588694.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/IBM_Warwick_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1588694.jpg/220px-IBM_Warwick_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1588694.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/IBM_Warwick_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1588694.jpg/440px-IBM_Warwick_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1588694.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="427" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:IBM_Warwick_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1588694.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>IBM at Warwick</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Aga_Rangemaster_Group" title="Aga Rangemaster Group">Aga Rangemaster Group</a> is on the north of Leamington Spa Business Park, and directly south is <a href="/wiki/Wolseley_UK" title="Wolseley UK">Wolseley UK</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Gruppo_Raicam&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gruppo Raicam (page does not exist)">Raicam Clutches</a> (<a href="/wiki/Automotive_Products" title="Automotive Products">Automotive Products</a>) is south of Wolseley; to the west <a href="/wiki/Grupo_Antolin" title="Grupo Antolin">Grupo Antolin</a> UK make vehicle interiors; on the same estate is Caparo AP Braking, and <a href="/wiki/Delphi_Automotive" class="mw-redirect" title="Delphi Automotive">Delphi Automotive</a> have an electronics centre. On the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Warwick_Technology_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Warwick Technology Park (page does not exist)">Warwick Technology Park</a>, south of Warwick on the <a href="/wiki/A425_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A425 road">A425</a>, are <a href="/wiki/Phillips_66" title="Phillips 66">Phillips 66</a> UK (former ConocoPhillips) who own <a href="/wiki/Jet_(brand)" title="Jet (brand)">JET UK</a> (petrol); to the east is <a href="/wiki/McKesson_Corporation" title="McKesson Corporation">McKesson</a>\'s European HQ (who produce the software for the NHS\'s 1.4&#160;million employees\' payroll \xe2\x80\x93 the largest payroll in the UK),<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and to the west is Tulip (who produce <a href="/wiki/Spam_(food)" title="Spam (food)">SPAM</a>, with Plumrose and Danepak) in the UK and are owned by <a href="/wiki/Danish_Crown_AmbA" class="mw-redirect" title="Danish Crown AmbA">Danish Crown Group</a> \xe2\x80\x93 Europe\'s largest pork producer, near <a href="/wiki/Midcounties_Co-operative" title="Midcounties Co-operative">Midcounties Co-operative</a> which is next to the wireless division of <a href="/wiki/Arqiva" title="Arqiva">Arqiva</a>; <a href="/wiki/National_Grid_plc" title="National Grid plc">National Grid plc</a> is in the centre of the park, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Allinea&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Allinea (page does not exist)">Allinea</a> Software is at the Innovation Centre.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:NFU_Mutual_Headquarters,_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/NFU_Mutual_Headquarters%2C_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg/220px-NFU_Mutual_Headquarters%2C_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg" width="220" height="166" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/NFU_Mutual_Headquarters%2C_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg/330px-NFU_Mutual_Headquarters%2C_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/NFU_Mutual_Headquarters%2C_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg/440px-NFU_Mutual_Headquarters%2C_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="1510" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:NFU_Mutual_Headquarters,_Tiddington_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1727835.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>NFU Mutual headquarters at Tiddington, east of Stratford-upon-Avon</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/NFU_Mutual" title="NFU Mutual">NFU Mutual</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Tiddington,_Warwickshire" title="Tiddington, Warwickshire">Tiddington</a> near Stratford and the <a href="/wiki/National_Farmers_Union_(England_and_Wales)" class="mw-redirect" title="National Farmers Union (England and Wales)">NFU</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Stoneleigh,_Warwickshire" title="Stoneleigh, Warwickshire">Stoneleigh</a>; <a href="/wiki/The_Pony_Club" title="The Pony Club">The Pony Club</a> and other parts of the <a href="/wiki/British_Equestrian_Federation" title="British Equestrian Federation">British Equestrian Federation</a> are in Stoneleigh. <a href="/wiki/AGCO" title="AGCO">AGCO</a> Limited UK and its European Operations Centre is nearby at <a href="/wiki/Stareton" title="Stareton">Stareton</a>, who own <a href="/wiki/Massey_Ferguson" title="Massey Ferguson">Massey Ferguson</a> with <a href="/wiki/Valtra" title="Valtra">Valtra</a> UK; the large factory at Coventry closed in 2002. The <a href="/wiki/British_Horse_Society" title="British Horse Society">British Horse Society</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Kenilworth" title="Kenilworth">Kenilworth</a>. At <a href="/wiki/Cubbington" title="Cubbington">Cubbington</a> is the UK headquarters of <a href="/wiki/Joma" title="Joma">Joma</a>, and has the Thwaites <a href="/wiki/Dumper" title="Dumper">dumper</a> manufacturer. <a href="/wiki/Caparo_Vehicle_Technologies" title="Caparo Vehicle Technologies">Caparo Vehicle Technologies</a> is off the <a href="/wiki/B4087_road" class="mw-redirect" title="B4087 road">B4087 road</a> towards Leamington Spa. <a href="/wiki/Codemasters" title="Codemasters">Codemasters</a> is off the A425 in <a href="/wiki/Long_Itchington" title="Long Itchington">Long Itchington</a>, east of Leamington, opposite the 600-acre <a href="/w/index.php?title=RLS_Polo_Club&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="RLS Polo Club (page does not exist)">RLS Polo Club</a>; directly east of Leamington on the A425 is Ricardo\'s <a href="/w/index.php?title=Midlands_Technical_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Midlands Technical Centre (page does not exist)">Midlands Technical Centre</a>. <a href="/wiki/Recaro" title="Recaro">Recaro</a> UK (car seats) is off the <a href="/wiki/A4177_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A4177 road">A4177</a> next to a <a href="/wiki/RAF_Honiley" title="RAF Honiley">former airfield</a> (now a proving ground), west of Kenilworth. Further north, the University of Warwick, on the Coventry/Warwickshire boundary, is home to the <a href="/wiki/WMG_(formerly_Warwick_Manufacturing_Group)" class="mw-redirect" title="WMG (formerly Warwick Manufacturing Group)">Warwick Manufacturing Group</a> technology consultancy and the <a href="/wiki/Tata_Motors" title="Tata Motors">Tata Motors</a> European Technical Centre.\n</p><p><a href="/w/index.php?title=SRS_Frigadon&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="SRS Frigadon (page does not exist)">SRS Frigadon</a>, off the <a href="/wiki/A3400_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A3400 road">A3400</a> (former A34) at <a href="/wiki/Atherstone_on_Stour" title="Atherstone on Stour">Atherstone on Stour</a>, is an Anglo-Swedish refrigeration company that makes <a href="/wiki/Chiller" title="Chiller">chillers</a> and heat exchangers.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg/220px-Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg" width="220" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg/330px-Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg/440px-Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Entrance_to_Daw_Mill_Colliery_-_geograph.org.uk_-_210862.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>In 2008, the former <a href="/wiki/Daw_Mill" title="Daw Mill">Daw Mill</a> colliery produced 3.2&#160;million tonnes of coal, a UK record</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/BMW" title="BMW">BMW</a> have their main European <a href="/wiki/Straight-4" class="mw-redirect" title="Straight-4">four-cylinder engine</a> plant at <a href="/wiki/Hams_Hall" title="Hams Hall">Hams Hall</a> near the M42. <a href="/wiki/Subaru" title="Subaru">Subaru</a> UK and <a href="/wiki/Isuzu" class="mw-redirect" title="Isuzu">Isuzu</a> UK (IM Group) are sandwiched between the M6 and the M42 (south of junction 8) at the Coleshill Manor Office Campus, west of <a href="/wiki/Coleshill,_Warwickshire" title="Coleshill, Warwickshire">Coleshill</a>. Off the B4117 in the north of Coleshill is <a href="/wiki/Thomas_%26_Betts" title="Thomas &amp; Betts">Thomas &amp; Betts</a> UK (former <a href="/w/index.php?title=Adaptaflex&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Adaptaflex (page does not exist)">Adaptaflex</a>), which makes <a href="/wiki/Electrical_conduit" title="Electrical conduit">flexible conduits</a>. <a href="/wiki/TNT_N.V." title="TNT N.V.">TNT</a> UK is off the B4116 in the west of <a href="/wiki/Atherstone" title="Atherstone">Atherstone</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Aldi" title="Aldi">Aldi</a> UK is on the other side of the road; Aldi opened its first UK store on 17 July 1990 in Stechford, Birmingham, and now has around 700 UK stores. <a href="/wiki/3M" title="3M">3M</a> have an <a href="/wiki/Abrasive" title="Abrasive">abrasive</a> products (<a href="/wiki/Sandpaper" title="Sandpaper">sandpaper</a>) factory in the east of the town. <a href="/wiki/Daw_Mill" title="Daw Mill">Daw Mill</a>, next to the <a href="/wiki/Birmingham_to_Peterborough_Line" class="mw-redirect" title="Birmingham to Peterborough Line">railway</a>, was Britain\'s biggest coal producer near the B4098/B4114 junction at <a href="/wiki/Arley,_Warwickshire" title="Arley, Warwickshire">Arley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Over_Whitacre" title="Over Whitacre">Over Whitacre</a>. <a href="/wiki/Holland_%26_Barrett" title="Holland &amp; Barrett">Holland &amp; Barrett</a> are Europe\'s largest health food chain, with 1,400 stores.  <a href="/wiki/Triton_Showers" title="Triton Showers">Triton Showers</a> (the UK\'s largest shower company) are based in <a href="/wiki/Nuneaton" title="Nuneaton">Nuneaton</a>; <a href="/wiki/Adams_Childrenswear" class="mw-redirect" title="Adams Childrenswear">Adams Childrenswear</a>, formerly on the A4254 on the <a href="/wiki/Attleborough,_Warwickshire" title="Attleborough, Warwickshire">Attleborough</a> Fields Ind Est, closed most of its stores in 2010.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2018)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>South of Nuneaton, at the <a href="/wiki/A444_road" title="A444 road">A444</a>/B4113 roundabout is the national distribution centre of <a href="/wiki/Dairy_Crest" title="Dairy Crest">Dairy Crest</a>, where it also packages <a href="/wiki/Cathedral_City_Cheddar" title="Cathedral City Cheddar">Cathedral City</a> cheese. North of Coventry, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Oleo_International&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Oleo International (page does not exist)">Oleo International</a> (its name is from the <a href="/wiki/Oleo_strut" title="Oleo strut">Oleo strut</a>) is a world leader in <a href="/wiki/Buffer_(rail_transport)" title="Buffer (rail transport)">railway buffers</a> based on the B4113 in <a href="/wiki/Exhall" title="Exhall">Exhall</a>, next to the M6. The <a href="/wiki/London_congestion_charge" title="London congestion charge">London congestion charge</a> is operated by Capita, based at Prologis Park (Bedworth) in the west of Exhall. <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_plc" class="mw-redirect" title="Rolls-Royce plc">Rolls-Royce</a> have a large engine overhaul plant (former <a href="/wiki/Armstrong_Siddeley" title="Armstrong Siddeley">Armstrong Siddeley</a>), near <a href="/wiki/Ansty,_Warwickshire" title="Ansty, Warwickshire">Ansty</a> and the M6/M69 junction in <a href="/wiki/Coombe_Fields" class="mw-redirect" title="Coombe Fields">Coombe Fields</a>, which also makes their engine casings, built on a <a href="/wiki/RAF_Ansty" title="RAF Ansty">former airfield</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ansty_Park&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ansty Park (page does not exist)">Ansty Park</a> is a new development on the same former airfield.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Aston_Martin" title="Aston Martin">Aston Martin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Land_Rover_Gaydon_Centre" title="Jaguar Land Rover Gaydon Centre">Land Rover</a> have their headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Gaydon" title="Gaydon">Gaydon</a>. Nearby to the south in the same area as the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Edgehill" title="Battle of Edgehill">Battle of Edgehill</a> (1642) west of the M40 is <a href="/wiki/MoD_Kineton" title="MoD Kineton">MoD Kineton</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Defence_Storage_and_Distribution_Agency" title="Defence Storage and Distribution Agency">Defence Storage and Distribution Agency</a> or DSDA Kineton, now part of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Equipment_and_Support" title="Defence Equipment and Support">Defence Equipment and Support</a> or DE&amp;S), home of the Army School of Ammunition and <a href="/wiki/Defence_Explosive_Ordnance_Disposal,_Munitions_and_Search_Training_Regiment" title="Defence Explosive Ordnance Disposal, Munitions and Search Training Regiment">Defence Explosive Ordnance Disposal, Munitions and Search Training Regiment</a> which teaches <a href="/wiki/Bomb_disposal" title="Bomb disposal">bomb disposal</a> (Improvised Explosive Device Disposal); on the opposite site of the B4086 is <a href="/w/index.php?title=Marlborough_Barracks&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Marlborough Barracks (page does not exist)">Marlborough Barracks</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Defence_Munitions_Centre&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Defence Munitions Centre (page does not exist)">Defence Munitions Centre</a> Kineton.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg/220px-Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg/330px-Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg/440px-Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Rugby-Millbuck_House_-_geograph.org.uk_-_1012751.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Morgan Sindall Construction HQ on Corporation Street (B4632) in Rugby</div></div></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/GE_Power_Conversion" title="GE Power Conversion">GE Power Conversion</a> UK (former Alstom, then Converteam) and <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Sindall" class="mw-redirect" title="Morgan Sindall">Morgan Sindall</a> Construction &amp; Infrastructure (former <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Est" title="Morgan Est">Morgan Est</a>) are in <a href="/wiki/Rugby,_Warwickshire" title="Rugby, Warwickshire">Rugby</a>. <a href="/wiki/Alstom" title="Alstom">Alstom</a> have their Power and Transport division in the north of Rugby on the <a href="/wiki/A426_road" title="A426 road">A426</a>, where they service <a href="/wiki/Steam_turbine" title="Steam turbine">steam turbines</a>; on the Swift Valley Ind Estate <a href="/wiki/Premier_Foods" title="Premier Foods">Premier Foods</a> have their national distribution centre; on the same estate <a href="/wiki/Ball_Corporation" title="Ball Corporation">Ball Packaging Europe</a> UK have a main plant (<a href="/wiki/Tin_can" title="Tin can">tin cans</a>), and nearby are <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mors%C3%B8_(company)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Mors\xc3\xb8 (company) (page does not exist)">Mors\xc3\xb8</a> UK (<a href="/wiki/Wood-burning_stove" title="Wood-burning stove">wood-burning stoves</a>). The European HQ of <a href="/wiki/Gap_(clothing_retailer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Gap (clothing retailer)">Gap</a> is in the north of Rugby, alongside the M6 in <a href="/wiki/Churchover" title="Churchover">Churchover</a>; Gap is the world\'s third-biggest fashion retailer, with 118 stores in the UK. <a href="/wiki/CEMEX" class="mw-redirect" title="CEMEX">CEMEX</a> have the country\'s largest cement works, west of Rugby at the junction of the A428 and the <a href="/wiki/A4071_road" class="mw-redirect" title="A4071 road">A4071</a> western bypass towards <a href="/wiki/Long_Lawford" title="Long Lawford">Long Lawford</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Rugby_Cement" class="mw-redirect" title="Rugby Cement">Rugby Cement</a>).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" Africa, made in Solihull</div></div></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Forensic_Science_Service" title="Forensic Science Service">Forensic Science Service</a>, <a href="/wiki/Linpac" title="Linpac">Linpac</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lafarge_(company)" title="Lafarge (company)">Lafarge Cement UK</a> and <a href="/wiki/IMI_plc" title="IMI plc">IMI plc</a> (former <a href="/wiki/ICI_Metals_Division" class="mw-redirect" title="ICI Metals Division">ICI Metals Division</a>) are on the Birmingham Business Park in <a href="/wiki/Bickenhill" title="Bickenhill">Bickenhill</a>, near the airport; the <a href="/wiki/National_Exhibition_Centre" title="National Exhibition Centre">National Exhibition Centre</a> (NEC) is just north, between the airport and the M42. <a href="/wiki/Lafarge_Tarmac" class="mw-redirect" title="Lafarge Tarmac">Lafarge Tarmac</a> is in Marston Green, <a href="/wiki/Bickenhill" title="Bickenhill">Bickenhill</a>; <a href="/wiki/ZF_Friedrichshafen" title="ZF Friedrichshafen">ZF Lemf\xc3\xb6rder UK</a>\'s site at Bickenhill makes axle modules for Land Rover off the B4438 north of the NEC, near the new site of <a href="/wiki/Tarmac_(company)" title="Tarmac (company)">Tarmac</a> (after the Lafarge merger). <a href="/wiki/Newey_and_Eyre" title="Newey and Eyre">Newey and Eyre</a>, Britain\'s largest electrical wholesaler and part of <a href="/wiki/Rexel" title="Rexel">Rexel</a> UK, is at Sheldon on the <a href="/wiki/A45_road" title="A45 road">A45</a> near the airport. <a href="/wiki/Neopost" title="Neopost">Neopost</a> UK is off the A452. <a href="/wiki/Goodrich_Corporation" title="Goodrich Corporation">Goodrich UK</a> is in <a href="/wiki/Shirley,_West_Midlands" title="Shirley, West Midlands">Shirley</a>. <a href="/wiki/Prologis" title="Prologis">Prologis</a> UK, <a href="/wiki/Intersport" title="Intersport">Intersport</a> UK (on the Cranmore Ind Est), and <a href="/wiki/Enterprise_Inns" class="mw-redirect" title="Enterprise Inns">Enterprise Inns</a> are on the A34 in <a href="/wiki/Monkspath" title="Monkspath">Monkspath</a>; next door is <a href="/wiki/Trelleborg_Sealing_Solutions" class="mw-redirect" title="Trelleborg Sealing Solutions">Trelleborg Sealing Solutions</a> UK; <a href="/wiki/TRW_Automotive" title="TRW Automotive">TRW Conekt</a> have a main automotive engineering research centre (with Girling Brakes, at the former Lucas Research Centre) at the A34/B4102 roundabout at The Green Business Park in Shirley Heath, further north on the A34 from Enterprise Inns, on other side of the road. The Mormons (Latter Day Saints) have their European HQ in Solihull near the <a href="/wiki/Heart_of_England_NHS_Foundation_Trust" title="Heart of England NHS Foundation Trust">hospital</a>, on the B4025 opposite Morrisons. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Amtico&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Amtico (page does not exist)">Amtico</a> (flooring) is based in the south of Solihull, with a main factory in <a href="/wiki/Foleshill" title="Foleshill">Foleshill</a>, Coventry. <a href="/w/index.php?title=Compin&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Compin (page does not exist)">Compin</a> UK, with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Fainsa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Fainsa (page does not exist)">Fainsa</a>, are in Solihull, and make train and bus seats.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Former_Staffordshire_Building_Society_Offices.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>\n<a href="/wiki/Tarmac_Group" title="Tarmac Group">Tarmac Group</a> was on the A4039 south-east of the city centre in <a href="/wiki/Ettingshall" title="Ettingshall">Ettingshall</a> until 2012 when it merged with Lafarge. <a href="/wiki/Marston%27s_Brewery" title="Marston&#39;s Brewery">Marston\'s</a> is headquartered west of the ring road, on the A41, and have the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Park_Brewery&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Park Brewery (page does not exist)">Park Brewery</a> on the A4124, east of the city centre. The UK\'s <a href="/w/index.php?title=VAT_Registration_Service&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="VAT Registration Service (page does not exist)">VAT Registration Service</a>, for <a href="/wiki/Value_Added_Tax_(United_Kingdom)" class="mw-redirect" title="Value Added Tax (United Kingdom)">Value Added Tax</a> is at HMRC in Wolverhampton on the opposite side of the <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Ring_Road" title="Wolverhampton Ring Road">Wolverhampton Ring Road</a> (A4150) to the HQ of Marstons, on the west side of the town centre. <a href="/wiki/Flint_Group" title="Flint Group">Flint Ink</a> UK in the east of the town centre, former <a href="/wiki/Mander_Brothers" title="Mander Brothers">Mander Brothers</a>, was the largest ink supplier in the <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a>, before being bought in 1998. <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems_Land_%26_Armaments" title="BAE Systems Land &amp; Armaments">BAE Systems Land &amp; Armaments</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Alvis_plc" title="Alvis plc">Alvis</a> Bridging and Vickers Armstrong) formerly on the A4126 in <a href="/wiki/Ettingshall" title="Ettingshall">Ettingshall</a>, near the former Tarmac site, closed at the end of 2011. In <a href="/wiki/Fordhouses" title="Fordhouses">Fordhouses</a>, along the <a href="/wiki/A449_road" title="A449 road">A449</a> to the north, are <a href="/w/index.php?title=HS_Marston&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="HS Marston (page does not exist)">HS Marston</a> (part of the former <a href="/wiki/Hamilton_Sundstrand" title="Hamilton Sundstrand">Hamilton Sundstrand</a>, now <a href="/wiki/UTC_Aerospace_Systems" title="UTC Aerospace Systems">UTC Aerospace Systems</a>) makes <a href="/wiki/Heat_exchanger" title="Heat exchanger">heat exchangers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goodrich_Corporation" title="Goodrich Corporation">Goodrich Actuation Systems</a> (the former Actuation Division of Lucas Aerospace and <a href="/w/index.php?title=H._M._Hobson&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="H. M. Hobson (page does not exist)">H. M. Hobson</a>), and a new engine plant for JLR. Goodrich in the UK, is what became of Lucas before a takeover by Goodrich; Lucas Aerospace was a world leader in flight control actuation for civil aircraft.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Steel_Distribution_Depot_-_geograph.org.uk_-_236054.jpg" class="image"><img alt=""
